giai_pt = function(a, b, c) {
if (a == 0) {
if (b == 0 & c == 0) {
print("PT vo so nghiem")
} else if (b == 0 & c != 0) {
print("PT vo nghiem")
} else {
print("PT c√≥ nghiem la: ")
print( (-c / b))
}
} else {
del = b * b - (4 * a * c)
if (del < 0) {
print("PT vo nghiem")
} else if (del == 0) {
print("PT co 1 nghiem kep")
print(-b / (2 * a))
} else {
print("PT co 2 nghiem phan biet")
print((-b + sqrt(del)) / 2 * a)
print((-b - sqrt(del)) / 2 * a)
}
}
}
x <- 0
y <- 2
z <- -3
giai_pt(x, y, z)

for (x in list(6,10,15,28,71,496)) {
n = x
i = 1
s = 0

while (i < n) {
if (n %% i == 0) {
s = s + i
}
i = i + 1
}
if (s == n) {
print(paste(n,"la so hoan thien"))
} else{
print(paste(n,"Khong la so hoan thien"))
}
}

function getObjectKey(obj, keys) {
for (let key in obj) {
if (typeof obj[key] == 'object') {
keys.push(key)
getObjectKey(obj[key], keys)
} else {
keys.push(key)
}
}
return keys;
}

result = []
const apartment = {

type: 'twin-bed',

}
}
}
